LIFE LESSONS.  The invaders entered the bank, and the eldest shouted at the insiders, "Don't move! The money belongs to the state, and the soul belongs to you!"  The people in the bank quickly fell to the ground. This is called a "distraction" - a distraction from ordinary thoughts.  A woman was lying on the table, and the mob shouted at her, "Ma'am! It's not violence here, it's theft. Lie down!"  It's called "skill" - just do what you love!  When the assailants finished their work and left the bank, the young, inexperienced thief asked the gang leader, "Can't we count how much we stole?" When can we count that much money? They will tell us later how much we stole on TV. "  This is called "experience" - today, life experience is more important than formal skills on paper.  As soon as the thieves left the bank, the bank's manager ordered an employee to call the police immediately. But the worker looked at his boss and said, "Stop! Let's take another 10 million and add it to the 70 million we closed yesterday."  This is called "swimming in the current" - any difficulty can be turned to its advantage.  The worker again dreamed, "Oh, every month there is such a theft."  This is called "fun" - the mood of work is more important than work.  A day passed. It was reported on TV that 100 million had been stolen from the bank. The thieves counted their money in disbelief: it was only 20 million.  "We risked our lives to get only 20 million. In the blink of an eye, the head of the bank died 80 million! It would be better for me to be an educated thief than a thief like that!"  This is called "knowledge is wealth." An engineer in Qiqihar City, Heilongjiang Province died on May 20, 2021, a year after he was released from serving a second prison term for practicing Falun Gong, a mind and body improvement system persecuted in China in the past 22 years.   Because of the relentless tortures in the prisons, Mr. Li Shunjiang suffered severe pleural effusion with excessive fluid buildup in his lungs and chest cavity. He could barely breathe. Instead of recovering, his health continued to decline, as he had to take care of his mentally ill wife and paralyzed mother-in-law, both of whom are also victims of the persecution. In addition to the constant police harassment, he eventually succumbed to the mental and physical distress. He was in his early 50s.   As his death was very sudden, his parents and sisters did not get to see him before he died.   In addition to his second prison term of three years, Mr. Li had previously served nine years in prison for his faith. Because he refused to renounce Falun Gong, he suffered a variety of tortures, including being hung up from handcuffs for a long time, long term sitting in a metal chair, beatings, beaten with metal clubs, solitary confinement, and force-feeding.
